hey guys,Im Gab.:) Thank u for supporting us all the way long. Yalu is kinda busy these days so im in charge now to update the story. There might be a couple spelling mistakes inside and i beg ur pardon :) -------------------------- l arrived in malpensa, first thing i looked at the screen for the time and the gate of my plane because it was the first time i take a plane on my own and I was pretty nervous but excited.I was carryng my baggage to a place where to sit because i arrived way too early, around 4 hours before my departure.. Waiting for my check in i didnt get bored at all, i kept watching the airplanes leaving and arriving, people going and people coming, the longer i was waiting the more excited i became,and finally the screen of my airline company was on. I went in the row and i hoped that everything was ok with my visa and documents or that my baggage was with the right weight. I know my worries was too exaggerated but it was the first time to do a long plane trip to the other side of the world and i couldnt do any mistake because i didnt want to appear like an idiot in front of yalu. After i get my boarding pass i runned to the screen to check my gate, it wasen't out so i asked to an hostess for explains and she said to dont worry too much and that it would be out soon. I remember i was hungry but i didnt have any food because i ate it all during the 4 hours i was waiting for the check in and i was too far from the snack bar or any food shop, so after i have found my gate i sit on the benches near the door of the tube for the airplanes and i waited there so i took my phone and proud of myself i sent a message to yalu: "Im in the gate waiting for the plane :)". My plane was directed to moscow and subsequently to guangzhou, it was 14.30 and i was giving my boarding pass to the hostess ready to leave. I get in the plane and it was not that big, 3 sits for side,so i reach mine,sit, and wait to take off. I had a couple sitting next to me, and i was imaging how wanderful should be if yalun was there with me, travel together to her hometown, know her family and her culture. Thinking of that i lost my mind and i start to image how it will be after i arrive, how is china, how are her parents, if they will like me and accept me, if i will like chinese food and so on. I was too happy and positive to be worry, then i thought that of course everything will be amazing but most importan i will be amazing and her parents will like me.( just to convince myself) The hostess was speaking at the microphone and in few minutes the plane was already up in the sky. While the take off i felt the sensation cause from taking off and it was intense, i ve almost forget that feeling since my last plane trip years ago. I was full of a strange energy, something that keeps me so awake, everything was so great even my apple juice was so great and i was feeling somwthing important, doing something out of ordinary like in the movies, i was relaxed and euphoric. I also tried to image how yalu should feel and i tried to think as her if she was excited as me. The 3 hours passed really fast and i was in Moscow international airport. It was a little complicate, Moscow airport is really big and i had to run to reach the right terminal in time. The gate was written on the screen but somehow it was wrong so i had to ask many times to find the right one and i was still not sure about it because it wasen't written anywhere. I was careful and paying super attenction to any eventual annunce about my plane. I get a bit worry in that situation, i was pretty sure i was in the right gate but many people there keep asking if it was for real the gate of the plane to guangzhou and it was giving me doubts. I met a woman, she was with her little daughter and she asked if it was the gate for guangzhou and i said that i was almost sure about that, we kept looking around and asking. After few minutes we saw that on the screen our plane number and i calm down and sit to wait. The woman asked me if i can look for her girl and baggage while she s going to the toilet, i was surprised about the trust she gave me ,i mean that place was so crowded and i could be a phsicopatic, but in fact she trusted me and she went to the toilet without problems. After she come back we started to talk, about why i was going to china and i asked it back, i said it was my first time and that i was going to my girlfriend, my girlfriend, i was so proud saying that, i even show her the picture of yalu in my wallet. The gate was open and after boarding i helped her with the baggage.Once in the plane i said goodbye and i went to find my sit. This plane unlike the previous one was bigger, i was in the middle , and at the start i had no people sit next to me and this was good but not for long.. in a short time the airplane get full and i had no extra space than my own. The pink ray of light from the russian sunset was lighting my face while the captain was ready to take off, i thought was better to sleep so after i arrive i would have an acceptable face and not looking like a zombie but i was too excited to sleep so i decided to take my ipod and listen to some music. 9 hours was long and i tried to be as more confortable as i can, and it was pretty easy, thinking about im going to yalun is enough to feel confortable even in the bulk of the plane, it was only to close my eyes and relax . The music helped my mind to dream and my body to relax and rest, everything i had to do was done, i didnt have to hope to don t miss the next plane because actually there was not a next plane. I was directed to Guangzhou, and only 9 hours separate me from that. I wished myself a good trip and i felt alseep between my wanderful dreams. When i woke up we were already in China, but still didnt arrive to Guangzhou airport, i tried to look out from the window but it was far from me and i couldnt see anything than clouds, i was in china!!! Happy as a child i look around , most of the passengers was chinese and everyone was sleeping, i was thinking " how can they sleep?? isnt it exciting?? come on we r in china!!" like i would be excited to take a train to go to my city, nevermind...for me was the most exciting thing. The captain ,as the take off ,lands on the course perfectly, really gently and quiet , so quiet that some people didnt even wake up but from their phone reciving messages . People starts to get their baggage and i was standing in the corridor waiting for them, hurry to get out, hurry to breathe the chinese air. Once we get out we were not really out so i couldnt feel the air because we were still in the tube and we directly enter in the airport but i felt the air was different anyway. I felt strongly to be in another world, i was so happy and i wanted to hug the man in front of the gate door, i wanted to hug everyone and say that i was so happy and honored to be in their wanderful land. Every step i do i can see how different it was from Europe, i remember the first thing i thought was: "Here they play serious". Everything was in a sistematic order and everyone had his job. I know europe has also rules and order but, there was different. I arrived to the acceptance and a worker check all my documents, a weird quiet was around me and the entire super big area, probably because everyone was tired from the trip but it was anyway something singular. After all my documents and face cheecking i went to take back my baggage, i found it really fast, i was walking down and first thing i saw on the tapisroulant was exactly my red baggage. Now the only thing to do was to go to my beloved yalu. I was walking in the corridor and i arrived in the area where the people waits for the passengers and as i always saw in the movies it was full of people holding a paper with the name of the person they r searching for, walking in that corridor with thousands people stare at u was something new, but i was staring back searching for my yalu. I kept walking with my eyes open, looking any where but when i saw her she already saw me and she were smiling, i runned and kiss her passionately.It was a long wanderful kiss, hugging my love and kissing , the only thing i wanted, i felt complete i felt also that feeling like the feeling u feel lying on a bed after a long day of work.With that kiss she gived me energy and power, and i felt fresh like i didnt do any long trip. Then i asked if she was waiting since too long and i suddenly remember about something... wtf i kissed her in that way and her parents could be everywhere.. so worry about that i immediately asked where they was, i was so worry that as first impression her parents sees me kissing her daughter before to say hello to them, when i saw her i completly forget about everything.. luckly she said that they was waiting us somewhere near the exit of that area.从没觉得我的英语这么好过。。。。（捂脸）
